JUST BRIEFLY SERVICE COORDINATION IS THE CORE FUNCTION OF REGIONAL CENTERS AND THE MOST VISIBLE FUNCTION THEY PROVIDE. IT GOES FAR BEYOND BEING AN ELIGIBILITY WORKER FOR RESPITE OR OTHER SERVICES AND IS FUNDAMENTALLY ABOUT MAKING THE LIVES OF PEOPLE WITH DISABILITIES AND THEIR FAMILIES BETTER AND EASIER.
